                            style={{
                              background:
                                issue.type === "error"
                                  ? "#dc2626"
                                  : issue.type === "duplicate"
                                    ? "#7c3aed"
                                    : "#d97706",
                              color: "white",
                              padding: "2px 8px",
                              borderRadius: "4px",
                              fontSize: "0.75rem",
                              fontWeight: 600,
                            }}
                          >
                            {issue.type?.toUpperCase()}
                          </span>
                        </td>
                        <td
                          style={{
                            padding: "6px 10px",
                            border: "1px solid #fca5a5",
                            color: "#991b1b",
                          }}
                        >
                          {issue.message}
                        </td>
                        <td
                          style={{
                            padding: "6px 10px",
                            border: "1px solid #fca5a5",
                            color: "#065f46",
                          }}
                        >
                          {issue.fix}
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                    ))}
                  </tbody>
                </table>
              </div>
            )}

            {excelValidation?.canProceed && (
              <div>
                <div
                  style={{
                    display: "grid",
                    gridTemplateColumns: "repeat(4,1fr)",
                    gap: "0.75rem",
                    marginBottom: "1.5rem",
                  }}
                >
                  {[
                    [
                      "✅ Valid",
                      excelValidation.validCount,
                      "#059669",
                      "#d1fae5",
                      "#a7f3d0",
                    ],
                    [
                      "⚠ Warnings",
                      excelValidation.warningCount,
                      "#d97706",
                      "#fef3c7",
                      "#fde68a",
                    ],
                    [
                      "🔴 Errors",
                      excelValidation.errorCount,
                      "#dc2626",
                      "#fee2e2",
                      "#fca5a5",
                    ],
                    [
                      "🔶 Diffs",
                      excelValidation.diffCount,
                      "#b45309",
                      "#fff7ed",
                      "#fed7aa",
                    ],
                  ].map(([label, count, color, bg, border]) => (
                    <div
                      key={label}
                      style={{
                        textAlign: "center",
                        padding: "1rem",
                        borderRadius: "10px",
                        background: bg,
                        border: `2px solid ${border}`,
                      }}
                    >
                      <div
                        style={{ fontSize: "1.6rem", fontWeight: 700, color }}
                      >
                        {count}
                      </div>
                      <div
                        style={{
                          fontSize: "0.78rem",
                          fontWeight: 600,
                          color,
                          marginTop: 2,
                        }}
                      >
                        {label}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>

                {diffIssues.length > 0 && (
                  <div
                    style={{
                      background: "#fff7ed",
                      border: "2px solid #f97316",
                      borderRadius: "12px",
                      padding: "1.25rem",
                      marginBottom: "1.5rem",
                    }}
                  >
                    <h4
                      style={{
                        margin: "0 0 1rem",
                        color: "#9a3412",
                        fontSize: "1rem",
                        fontWeight: 700,
                      }}
                    >
                      🔶 {diffIssues.length} Amount Mismatch
                      {diffIssues.length > 1 ? "es" : ""} — Must Approve Each
                    </h4>
                    {diffIssues.map((issue, i) => (
                      <div
                        key={i}
                        style={{
                          background: approvedDiffs.has(issue.memberId)
                            ? "#f0fdf4"
                            : "#fff",
                          border: `2px solid ${approvedDiffs.has(issue.memberId) ? "#86efac" : "#f97316"}`,
                          borderRadius: "8px",
                          padding: "1rem",
                          marginBottom: "0.75rem",
                        }}
                      >
                        <div
                          style={{
                            display: "flex",
                            justifyContent: "space-between",
                            alignItems: "flex-start",
                            gap: "1rem",
                          }}
                        >
                          <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                            <div
                              style={{
                                fontWeight: 700,
                                color: "#7c2d12",
                                fontSize: "0.95rem",
                                marginBottom: "0.5rem",
                              }}
                            >
                              🏠 {issue.flat} — {issue.name}
                            </div>
                            <div
                              style={{
                                display: "grid",
                                gridTemplateColumns: "1fr 1fr 1fr",
                                gap: "0.5rem",
                                marginBottom: "0.75rem",
                              }}
                            >
                              {[
                                [
                                  "Excel Total",
                                  `₹${issue.excelTotal}`,
                                  "#dc2626",
                                ],
                                [
                                  "System Calc",
                                  `₹${issue.autoTotal}`,
                                  "#059669",
                                ],
                                [
                                  "Difference",
                                  `₹${issue.diff > 0 ? "+" : ""}${issue.diff}`,
                                  issue.diff < 0 ? "#dc2626" : "#d97706",
                                ],
                              ].map(([l, v, c]) => (
                                <div
                                  key={l}
                                  style={{
                                    background: "#f9fafb",
                                    borderRadius: "6px",
                                    padding: "0.5rem",
                                    textAlign: "center",
                                    border: "1px solid #e5e7eb",
                                  }}
                                >
                                  <div
                                    style={{
                                      fontSize: "0.7rem",
                                      color: "#6b7280",
                                      marginBottom: "2px",
                                    }}
                                  >
                                    {l}
                                  </div>
                                  <div
                                    style={{
                                      fontSize: "1rem",
                                      fontWeight: 700,
                                      color: c,
                                    }}
                                  >
                                    {v}
                                  </div>
                                </div>
                              ))}
                            </div>
                            <div
                              style={{ fontSize: "0.8rem", color: "#92400e" }}
                            >
                              {issue.fix}
                            </div>
                          </div>
                          <label
                            style={{
                              display: "flex",
                              flexDirection: "column",
                              alignItems: "center",
                              gap: "4px",
                              cursor: "pointer",
                              minWidth: "80px",
                              textAlign: "center",
                              background: approvedDiffs.has(issue.memberId)
                                ? "#d1fae5"
                                : "#fee2e2",
                              border: `2px solid ${approvedDiffs.has(issue.memberId) ? "#059669" : "#dc2626"}`,
                              borderRadius: "8px",
                              padding: "0.75rem",
                            }}
                          >
                            <input
                              type="checkbox"
                              checked={approvedDiffs.has(issue.memberId)}
                              onChange={(e) => {
                                setApprovedDiffs((prev) => {
                                  const next = new Set(prev);
                                  e.target.checked
                                    ? next.add(issue.memberId)
                                    : next.delete(issue.memberId);
                                  return next;
                                });
                              }}
                              style={{
                                width: 18,
                                height: 18,
                                cursor: "pointer",
                              }}
                            />
                            <span
                              style={{
                                fontSize: "0.7rem",
                                fontWeight: 700,
                                color: approvedDiffs.has(issue.memberId)
                                  ? "#059669"
                                  : "#dc2626",
                              }}
                            >
                              {approvedDiffs.has(issue.memberId)
                                ? "APPROVED"
                                : "APPROVE?"}
                            </span>
                          </label>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                    {!allDiffsApproved && (
                      <div
                        style={{
                          background: "#fef2f2",
                          border: "1px solid #fca5a5",
                          borderRadius: "8px",
                          padding: "0.75rem",
                          marginTop: "0.5rem",
                          fontSize: "0.8rem",
                          color: "#991b1b",
                          fontWeight: 600,
                          textAlign: "center",
                        }}
                      >
                        ❌ Generate blocked — approve all{" "}
                        {diffIssues.length - approvedDiffs.size} remaining
                        mismatch
                        {diffIssues.length - approvedDiffs.size > 1
                          ? "es"
                          : ""}{" "}
                        to unlock
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                )}

                {excelValidation.comparison?.filter((r) => !r.hasDiff).length >
                  0 && (
                  <div style={{ marginBottom: "1.5rem" }}>
                    <h4
                      style={{
                        margin: "0 0 0.75rem",
                        color: "#374151",
                        fontSize: "0.95rem",
                        fontWeight: 700,
                      }}
                    >
                      ✅ Matched Rows (
                      {
                        excelValidation.comparison.filter((r) => !r.hasDiff)
                          .length
                      }
                      )
                    </h4>
                    <div
                      style={{
                        overflowX: "auto",
                        maxHeight: 260,
                        overflowY: "auto",
                        border: "1px solid #e5e7eb",
                        borderRadius: "8px",
                      }}
                    >
                      <table
                        style={{
                          width: "100%",
                          borderCollapse: "collapse",
                          fontSize: "0.8rem",
                        }}
                      >
                        <thead
                          style={{
                            position: "sticky",
                            top: 0,
                            background: "#d1fae5",
                            zIndex: 1,
                          }}
                        >
                          <tr>
                            {[
                              "Flat",
                              "Member",
                              "Excel Total",
                              "Auto Total",
                              "Status",
                            ].map((h) => (
                              <th
                                key={h}
                                style={{
                                  padding: "8px 10px",
                                  border: "1px solid #a7f3d0",
                                  textAlign: h.includes("Total")
                                    ? "right"
                                    : "left",
                                  color: "#065f46",
                                  fontWeight: 700,
                                }}
                              >
                                {h}
                              </th>
                            ))}
                          </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody>
                          {excelValidation.comparison
                            .filter((r) => !r.hasDiff)
                            .map((row, i) => (
                              <tr
                                key={i}
                                style={{
                                  background: i % 2 === 0 ? "#fff" : "#f9fafb",
                                }}
                              >
                                <td
                                  style={{
                                    padding: "7px 10px",
                                    border: "1px solid #e5e7eb",
                                    fontWeight: 600,
                                  }}
                                >
                                  {row.flat}
                                </td>
                                <td
                                  style={{
                                    padding: "7px 10px",
                                    border: "1px solid #e5e7eb",
                                  }}
                                >
                                  {row.name}
                                </td>
                                <td
                                  style={{
                                    padding: "7px 10px",
                                    border: "1px solid #e5e7eb",
                                    textAlign: "right",
                                    fontWeight: 600,
                                  }}
                                >
                                  ₹{row.excelTotal.toFixed(2)}
                                </td>
                                <td
                                  style={{
                                    padding: "7px 10px",
                                    border: "1px solid #e5e7eb",
                                    textAlign: "right",
                                    color: "#6b7280",
                                  }}
                                >
                                  ₹{row.autoTotal.toFixed(2)}
                                </td>
                                <td
                                  style={{
                                    padding: "7px 10px",
                                    border: "1px solid #e5e7eb",
                                    textAlign: "center",
                                  }}
                                >
                                  <span
                                    style={{
                                      background: "#d1fae5",
                                      color: "#065f46",
                                      padding: "2px 10px",
                                      borderRadius: "12px",
                                      fontSize: "0.75rem",
                                      fontWeight: 700,
                                    }}
                                  >
                                    ✓ Match
                                  </span>
                                </td>
                              </tr>
                            ))}
                        </tbody>
                      </table>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}

                <div
                  style={{
                    display: "flex",
                    gap: "0.75rem",
                    alignItems: "center",
                    borderTop: "2px solid #e5e7eb",
                    paddingTop: "1.25rem",
                  }}
                >
                  <button
                    className="btn btn-secondary"
                    onClick={() => {
                      setExcelFile(null);
                      setExcelValidation(null);
                    }}
                  >
                    ← Re-upload
                  </button>
                  <button
                    className={`btn ${canGenerate ? "btn-success" : "btn-secondary"}`}
                    style={{
                      minWidth: 240,
                      opacity: canGenerate ? 1 : 0.5,
                      cursor: canGenerate ? "pointer" : "not-allowed",
                    }}
                    disabled={!canGenerate}
                    onClick={async () => {
                      if (
                        !confirm(
                          `Generate ${excelValidation.validCount} bills from Excel for ${periodLabel}?\n\n${diffIssues.length > 0 ? `⚠ You approved ${diffIssues.length} manual amount override(s).` : "All amounts match auto-calculation."}`,
                        )
                      )
                        return;
                      setExcelImporting(true);
                      try {
                        const res = await fetch(
                          "/api/billing/generate-from-excel",
                          {
                            method: "POST",
                            credentials: "include",
                            headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
                            body: JSON.stringify({
                              bills: excelValidation.bills,
                              billMonth,
                              billYear,
                              dueDate,
                            }),
                          },
                        );
                        const data = await res.json();
                        if (!data.success)
                          throw new Error(data.error || "Generation failed");
                        alert(
                          `✅ Generated ${data.count} bills successfully from Excel.`,
                        );
                        queryClient.invalidateQueries(["bills-list"]);
                        setExcelFile(null);
                        setExcelValidation(null);
                      } catch (e) {
                        alert("❌ Failed: " + e.message);
                      } finally {
                        setExcelImporting(false);
                      }
                    }}
                  >
                    {excelImporting
                      ? "⏳ Generating..."
                      : !canGenerate
                        ? `🔒 Approve ${diffIssues.length - approvedDiffs.size} Diff${diffIssues.length - approvedDiffs.size > 1 ? "s" : ""} to Unlock`
                        : `🚀 Generate ${excelValidation.validCount} Bills from Excel`}
                  </button>
                  {canGenerate && diffIssues.length > 0 && (
                    <span
                      style={{
                        fontSize: "0.8rem",
                        color: "#d97706",
                        fontWeight: 600,
                      }}
                    >
                      ⚠ {diffIssues.length} manual override
                      {diffIssues.length > 1 ? "s" : ""} approved
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* FLOW 2 — PAYMENT COLLECTION */}
      <div
        style={{
          background: "#fff",
          border: "2px solid #bbf7d0",
          borderRadius: "12px",
          marginBottom: "1.5rem",
          overflow: "hidden",
        }}
      >
        <div
          style={{
            background: "#f0fdf4",
            padding: "1rem 1.5rem",
            borderBottom: "1px solid #bbf7d0",
          }}
        >
          <h2 style={{ margin: 0, fontSize: "1.1rem", color: "#166534" }}>
            💳 Flow 2 — Payment Collection
          </h2>
          <p
            style={{ margin: "4px 0 0", fontSize: "0.8rem", color: "#16a34a" }}
          >
            Download payment template → admin fills AmountPaid/Method/Date →
            upload → system validates and records payments
          </p>
        </div>
        <div style={{ padding: "1.5rem" }}>
          {/* 2A: Download Payment Collection Template */}
          <div
            style={{
              background: "#f0fdf4",
              border: "1px solid #bbf7d0",
              borderRadius: "10px",
              padding: "1.25rem",
              marginBottom: "1.5rem",
            }}
          >
            <h3
              style={{
                margin: "0 0 0.5rem",
                fontSize: "0.95rem",
                color: "#166534",
              }}
            >
              2A — Download Payment Collection Template
            </h3>
            <p
              style={{
                margin: "0 0 0.75rem",
                fontSize: "0.8rem",
                color: "#6b7280",
                lineHeight: 1.5,
              }}
            >
              Pre-filled with: opening balances, bill totals, remaining due,
              already paid, bill status. Admin fills ONLY: AmountPaid,
              PaymentMethod, PaymentDate, Remarks.
            </p>
            <div
              style={{
                fontSize: "0.78rem",
                color: "#166534",
                background: "#dcfce7",
                borderRadius: "6px",
                padding: "0.5rem 0.75rem",
                marginBottom: "1rem",
              }}
            >
              <strong>Read-only:</strong> MemberId · Wing · FlatNo · OwnerName ·
              Month · Year · OpeningPrincipal · OpeningInterest · CurrentCharges
              · CurrentInterest · BillPrincipal · BillInterest · TotalBillDue ·
              AlreadyPaid · RemainingDue · BillStatus
              <br />
              <strong>Fill these:</strong> AmountPaid · PaymentMethod ·
              PaymentDate · Remarks
            </div>
            <button
              className="btn btn-success"
              disabled={!canDownload}
              onClick={downloadPaymentTemplate}
              style={{ opacity: canDownload ? 1 : 0.5 }}
            >
              📥 Download Payment Collection Template ({periodLabel})
              {selectedMemberIds.size > 0
                ? ` — ${selectedMemberIds.size} members`
                : ""}
            </button>
          </div>

          {/* 2B: Upload Payment Collection Template */}
          <div
            style={{
              background: "#f9fafb",
              border: "1px solid #e5e7eb",
              borderRadius: "10px",
              padding: "1.25rem",
            }}
          >
            <h3
              style={{
                margin: "0 0 0.5rem",
                fontSize: "0.95rem",
                color: "#374151",
              }}
            >
              2B — Upload Filled Payment Template
            </h3>
            <p
              style={{
                margin: "0 0 1rem",
                fontSize: "0.8rem",
                color: "#6b7280",
                lineHeight: 1.5,
              }}
            >
              Upload the filled payment template. System validates, previews
              allocations, then you confirm to post payments and generate
              receipts.
            </p>

            {!payPreview && !payResults && (
              <div
                style={{
                  display: "flex",
                  gap: "1rem",
                  alignItems: "flex-end",
                  flexWrap: "wrap",
                }}
              >
                <div>
                  <label
                    style={{
                      display: "block",
                      fontSize: "0.8rem",
                      color: "#374151",
                      marginBottom: 4,
                    }}
                  >
                    Filled Payment Template (.xlsx)
                  </label>
                  <input
                    type="file"
                    accept=".xlsx,.xls"
                    onChange={(e) => setPayFile(e.target.files?.[0] || null)}
                    style={{ fontSize: "0.875rem" }}
                  />
                </div>
                <button
                  className="btn btn-primary"
                  disabled={!payFile || payPreviewing}
                  onClick={handlePayPreview}
                >
                  {payPreviewing ? "⏳ Validating..." : "🔍 Validate & Preview"}
                </button>
              </div>
            )}

            {payGrid && (
              <ExcelPreviewGrid
                title={`Payment Template Preview — ${periodLabel}`}
                columns={payGrid.columns}
                rows={payGrid.gridRows}
                onReupload={() => {
                  setPayFile(null);
                  setPayPreview(null);
                  setPayBatchKey(null);
                  setPayGrid(null);
                  setPayResults(null);
                }}
                onContinue={(_validRows) => {
                  /* actual confirm uses handlePayConfirm button below */
                }}
                onCancel={() => {
                  setPayFile(null);
                  setPayPreview(null);
                  setPayBatchKey(null);
                  setPayGrid(null);
                  setPayResults(null);
                }}
              />
            )}

            {payPreview && (
              <div>
                <div
                  style={{
                    display: "grid",
                    gridTemplateColumns: "repeat(auto-fit, minmax(140px, 1fr))",
                    gap: "0.75rem",
                    marginBottom: "1rem",
                  }}
                >
                  {[
                    { label: "Total Rows", value: payPreview.totalRows },
                    {
                      label: "Valid",
                      value: payPreview.validRows,
                      color: "#059669",
                    },
                    {
                      label: "Errors",
                      value: payPreview.failedRows,
                      color: payPreview.failedRows > 0 ? "#dc2626" : undefined,
                    },
                    {
                      label: "Total Amount",
                      value: `₹${(payPreview.totalAmount || 0).toFixed(2)}`,
                    },
                  ].map(({ label, value, color }) => (
                    <div
                      key={label}
                      style={{
                        background: "#f9fafb",
                        borderRadius: 8,
                        padding: "0.75rem",
                        textAlign: "center",
                      }}
                    >
                      <div
                        style={{
                          fontSize: "1.4rem",
                          fontWeight: 700,
                          color: color || "#1f2937",
                        }}
                      >
                        {value}
                      </div>
                      <div style={{ fontSize: "0.75rem", color: "#6b7280" }}>
                        {label}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>

                {payPreview.errors?.length > 0 && (
                  <div
                    style={{
                      background: "#fef2f2",
                      border: "1px solid #fca5a5",
                      borderRadius: 8,
                      padding: "0.75rem",
                      marginBottom: "1rem",
                    }}
                  >
                    <strong style={{ color: "#dc2626" }}>Row Errors:</strong>
                    <ul
                      style={{
                        margin: "0.5rem 0 0",
                        paddingLeft: "1.25rem",
                        fontSize: "0.8rem",
                        color: "#7f1d1d",
                      }}
                    >
                      {payPreview.errors.map((e, i) => (
                        <li key={i}>
                          Row {e.rowNum}: {e.errors.join(", ")}
                        </li>
                      ))}
                    </ul>
                  </div>
                )}

                <div style={{ overflowX: "auto", marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
                  <table
                    style={{
                      width: "100%",
                      borderCollapse: "collapse",
                      fontSize: "0.8rem",
                    }}
                  >
                    <thead>
                      <tr style={{ background: "#f3f4f6" }}>
                        {[
                          "Row",
                          "Flat",
                          "Member",
                          "Period",
                          "Bill Due",
                          "Paying",
                          "Method",
                          "Date",
                          "Status",
                        ].map((h) => (
                          <th
                            key={h}
                            style={{
                              padding: "0.5rem 0.75rem",
                              textAlign: "left",
                              borderBottom: "1px solid #e5e7eb",
                              whiteSpace: "nowrap",
                            }}
                          >
                            {h}
                          </th>
                        ))}
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      {payPreview.preview.map((row, i) => (
                        <tr
                          key={i}
                          style={{
                            background:
                              row.status === "Failed"
                                ? "#fef2f2"
                                : i % 2 === 0
                                  ? "#fff"
                                  : "#f9fafb",
                          }}
                        >
                          <td style={{ padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem" }}>
                            {row.rowNum}
                          </td>
                          <td style={{ padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem" }}>
                            {row.flat}
                          </td>
                          <td style={{ padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem" }}>
                            {row.memberName}
                          </td>
                          <td style={{ padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem" }}>
                            {row.billPeriodId}
                          </td>
                          <td style={{ padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem" }}>
                            ₹{(row.remaining || 0).toFixed(2)}
                          </td>
                          <td
                            style={{
                              padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem",
                              fontWeight: 600,
                            }}
                          >
                            ₹{(row.amountPaid || 0).toFixed(2)}
                          </td>
                          <td style={{ padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem" }}>
                            {row.paymentMethod}
                          </td>
                          <td style={{ padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem" }}>
                            {row.paymentDate}
                          </td>
                          <td style={{ padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem" }}>
                            <span
                              style={{
                                color:
                                  row.status === "Valid"
                                    ? "#059669"
                                    : "#dc2626",
                                fontWeight: 600,
                              }}
                            >
                              {row.status === "Failed"
                                ? `❌ ${row.errors?.join(", ")}`
                                : "✅ Valid"}
                            </span>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                      ))}
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>

                <div
                  style={{ display: "flex", gap: "0.75rem", flexWrap: "wrap" }}
                >
                  <button
                    className="btn btn-success"
                    disabled={payPreview.validRows === 0 || payConfirming}
                    onClick={handlePayConfirm}
                  >
                    {payConfirming
                      ? "⏳ Processing..."
                      : `✅ Confirm & Process ${payPreview.validRows} Payment(s)`}
                  </button>
                  <button
                    className="btn btn-secondary"
                    onClick={() => {
                      setPayPreview(null);
                      setPayBatchKey(null);
                      setPayFile(null);
                    }}
                  >
                    ← Re-upload
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}

            {payResults && (
              <div>
                <div
                  style={{
                    background: "#f0fdf4",
                    border: "1px solid #86efac",
                    borderRadius: 8,
                    padding: "1rem",
                    marginBottom: "1rem",
                  }}
                >
                  <strong style={{ color: "#166534" }}>
                    ✅ Payments Processed
                  </strong>
                  <div
                    style={{
                      marginTop: "0.5rem",
                      fontSize: "0.875rem",
                      color: "#166534",
                    }}
                  >
                    {payResults.successRows} succeeded · {payResults.failedRows}{" "}
                    failed · Total ₹
                    {(payResults.totalAmountProcessed || 0).toFixed(2)} ·
                    Interest cleared ₹
                    {(payResults.totalInterestCleared || 0).toFixed(2)} ·
                    Principal cleared ₹
                    {(payResults.totalPrincipalCleared || 0).toFixed(2)}
                  </div>
                </div>
                {payResults.failedRows > 0 && (
                  <div style={{ overflowX: "auto", marginBottom: "1rem" }}>
                    <table
                      style={{
                        width: "100%",
                        borderCollapse: "collapse",
                        fontSize: "0.8rem",
                      }}
                    >
                      <thead>
                        <tr style={{ background: "#fef2f2" }}>
                          {["Flat", "Member", "Amount", "Error"].map((h) => (
                            <th
                              key={h}
                              style={{
                                padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem",
                                textAlign: "left",
                                borderBottom: "1px solid #fca5a5",
                              }}
                            >
                              {h}
                            </th>
                          ))}
                        </tr>
                      </thead>
                      <tbody>
                        {payResults.results
                          ?.filter((r) => r.status === "Failed")
                          .map((r, i) => (
                            <tr key={i}>
                              <td style={{ padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem" }}>
                                {r.flat}
                              </td>
                              <td style={{ padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem" }}>
                                {r.memberName}
                              </td>
                              <td style={{ padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem" }}>
                                ₹{(r.amountPaid || 0).toFixed(2)}
                              </td>
                              <td
                                style={{
                                  padding: "0.4rem 0.75rem",
                                  color: "#dc2626",
                                }}
                              >
                                {r.errorMessage}
                              </td>
                            </tr>
                          ))}
                      </tbody>
                    </table>
                  </div>
                )}
                <button
                  className="btn btn-secondary"
                  onClick={() => setPayResults(null)}
                >
                  Upload Another Batch
                </button>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Preview Modal */}
      {showPreview && previewData && currentBill && (
        <div className={styles.modal} onClick={() => setShowPreview(false)}>
          <div
            className={styles.modalContent}
            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            <div className={styles.modalHeader}>
              <div>
                <div
                  className={styles.modalHeader}
                  // or your existing header container
                >
                  <h2>Bill Preview - {currentBill.member}</h2>
                  {currentBill && (
                    <label
                      style={{
                        display: "flex",
                        alignItems: "center",
                        gap: 8,
                        fontSize: 13,
                      }}
                    >
                      <input
                        type="checkbox"
                        checked={isCurrentSelected}
                        onChange={(e) => {
                          setSelectedMemberIds((prev) => {
                            const next = new Set(prev);
                            if (e.target.checked)
                              next.add(currentBill.memberId);
                            else next.delete(currentBill.memberId);
                            return next;
                          });
                        }}
                      />
                      Include this member
                    </label>
                  )}
                </div>{" "}
                <p
                  style={{
                    margin: "5px 0 0 0",
                    color: "#6b7280",
                    fontSize: "0.95rem",
                  }}
                >
                  {currentBill.memberName} | {currentBill.area} sq ft
                  {currentBill.previousBalance > 0 && (
                    <span
                      style={{
                        color: "#dc2626",
                        fontWeight: "600",
                        marginLeft: "15px",
                      }}
                    >
                      ⚠️ Has Outstanding: ₹
                      {currentBill.previousBalance.toLocaleString("en-IN")}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </p>
              </div>
              <button
                onClick={() => setShowPreview(false)}
                className={styles.closeBtn}
              >
                ✕
              </button>
            </div>

            <div className={styles.modalBody}>
              <div
                dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{
                  __html: renderBillHTML(currentBill),
                }}
              />
            </div>

            <div className={styles.modalFooter}>
              <div className={styles.navigation}>
                <button
                  onClick={() => setPreviewIndex(Math.max(0, previewIndex - 1))}
                  disabled={previewIndex === 0}
                  className="btn btn-secondary"
                >
                  ← Previous
                </button>
                <span className={styles.pageInfo}>
                  <strong>{previewIndex + 1}</strong> of{" "}
                  <strong>{previewData.length}</strong>
                </span>
                <button
                  onClick={() =>
                    setPreviewIndex(
                      Math.min(previewData.length - 1, previewIndex + 1),
                    )
                  }
                  disabled={previewIndex === previewData.length - 1}
                  className="btn btn-secondary"
                >
                  Next →
                </button>
              </div>

              <button
                onClick={generateMutation.mutate}
                disabled={generateMutation.isPending}
                className="btn btn-success btn-lg"
                style={{ minWidth: 250 }}
              >
                {generateMutation.isPending ? (
                  <>
                    <span className="loading-spinner"></span>
                    {` Generating... ${genProgress.current}/${genProgress.total}`}
                    <div
                      style={{
                        marginTop: 6,
                        height: 4,
                        background: "#dbeafe",
                        borderRadius: 4,
                      }}
                    >
                      <div
                        style={{
                          width: `${genProgress.total ? (genProgress.current / genProgress.total) * 100 : 0}%`,
                          height: "100%",
                          background: "#1e40af",
                          borderRadius: 4,
                          transition: "width 0.3s ease",
                        }}
                      />
                    </div>
                  </>
                ) : (
                  `  Generate Bills for ${selectedMemberIds.size} member
  ${selectedMemberIds.size === 1 ? "" : "s"}`
                )}
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
</file>

<file path="middleware.js">
import { NextResponse } from "next/server";

export function middleware(request) {
  const { pathname } = request.nextUrl;

  const token = request.cookies.get("token")?.value;
  const adminToken = request.cookies.get("admin_token")?.value;

  function parseJwt(t) {
    try {
      const base64Url = t.split(".")[1];
      const base64 = base64Url.replace(/-/g, "+").replace(/_/g, "/");
      const jsonPayload = decodeURIComponent(
        atob(base64)
          .split("")
          .map((c) => "%" + ("00" + c.charCodeAt(0).toString(16)).slice(-2))
          .join(""),
      );
      return JSON.parse(jsonPayload);
    } catch {
      return null;
    }
  }

  // ✅ PUBLIC ROUTES
  const publicRoutes = [
    "/auth/login",
    "/auth/signup",
    "/admin/login",
    "/member/login",
    "/superadmin/login",
  ];
  if (publicRoutes.some((route) => pathname.startsWith(route))) {
    return NextResponse.next();
  }

  // ─── ROOT REDIRECT ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  if (pathname === "/") {
    // SuperAdmin: has adminToken, no token
    if (adminToken) {
      const adminPayload = parseJwt(adminToken);
      if (adminPayload?.role === "SuperAdmin") {
        return NextResponse.redirect(
          new URL("/superadmin/dashboard", request.url),
        );
      }
    }
    // Admin / Member: has token
    if (token) {
      const payload = parseJwt(token);
      if (payload?.role === "Admin" || payload?.role === "Secretary") {
        return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/admin/dashboard", request.url));
      }
      if (payload?.role === "Member") {
        return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/member/dashboard", request.url));
      }
    }
    return NextResponse.next();
  }

  // ─── SUPERADMIN ROUTES ───────────────────────────────────────────
  // Handled entirely via adminToken — never needs token
  if (pathname.startsWith("/superadmin")) {
    if (!adminToken) {
      return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/superadmin/login", request.url));
    }
    const adminPayload = parseJwt(adminToken);
    if (!adminPayload || adminPayload.role !== "SuperAdmin") {
      return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/superadmin/login", request.url));
    }
    return NextResponse.next();
  }

  // ─── ADMIN + MEMBER PROTECTED ROUTES ─────────────────────────────
  if (!token) {
    return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/auth/login", request.url));
  }

  const payload = parseJwt(token);
  if (!payload) {
    return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/auth/login", request.url));
  }

  const role = payload.role;

  // /admin exact → redirect to dashboard
  if (pathname === "/admin") {
    return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/admin/dashboard", request.url));
  }

  if (
    pathname.startsWith("/admin") &&
    role !== "Admin" &&
    role !== "Secretary"
  ) {
    return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/auth/login", request.url));
  }

  if (pathname.startsWith("/member") && role !== "Member") {
    return NextResponse.redirect(new URL("/auth/login", request.url));
  }

  return NextResponse.next();
}

export const config = {
  matcher: ["/", "/admin/:path*", "/member/:path*", "/superadmin/:path*"],
};
</file>

<file path="models/User.js">
import mongoose from "mongoose";

const UserSchema = new mongoose.Schema(
  {
    name: {
      type: String,
      required: true,
      trim: true,
    },
    email: {
      type: String,
      required: true,
      unique: true,
      lowercase: true,
      trim: true,
    },
    password: {
      type: String,
      required: true,
    },
    role: {
      type: String,
enum: ["SuperAdmin", "Admin", "Secretary", "Accountant", "Member"],      default: "Member",
    },
    societyId: {
      type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,
      ref: "Society",
      required: true,
    },
    memberId: {
      type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,
      ref: "Member",
      required: false,
    },
    isActive: {
      type: Boolean,
      default: true,
    },
  },
  {
    timestamps: true,
  }
);

export default mongoose.models.User || mongoose.model("User", UserSchema);
</file>
